# ZMN Roadmap

> **Single source of truth for all ZMN work items.** Last updated: 2026-04-22.
>
> All prior audit docs remain in `docs/audits/` as evidence and context; their
> actionable items are consolidated here. Update this roadmap at the end of every
> session that completes or changes an item's status. Append a changelog entry.
>
> Audit docs are linked in the **Source** column of each item below — open the
> audit for evidence; trust the roadmap for current status and priority.

## How to read this roadmap

**Status legend:** ✅ COMPLETED · 🟡 IN_PROGRESS · 📋 QUEUED · ⏸️ DEFERRED · ⛔ SUPERSEDED · ❓ UNKNOWN (needs verification)

**Tier semantics:**
- **Tier 1** — env-var / docs / single-file changes; low risk; ≤30 min sessions
- **Tier 2** — single-session MCP integrations or focused features; 30–180 min; medium risk
- **Tier 3** — multi-session projects; high scope; coordinated across weeks
- **Tier 4** — prerequisites that gate other tiers (handle first)

**ID scheme:** `TUNE-*` trading tuning · `DOCS-*` documentation · `OBS-*` observability · `INFRA-*` infrastructure · `DASH-*` dashboard structure · `DASH-B-*` specific dashboard bugs · `DASH-ENTRY-*` bot_core entry-path writes feeding dashboard · `ML-*` model · `WHALE-*` smart-money · `MCP-*` MCP-build candidates · `LIVE-*` live-trading enablement · `SEC-*` security · `BUG-*` other known bugs · `CLEAN-*` cleanup · `TG-*` telegram · `REFACTOR-*` refactors (multi-session, pure hygiene) · `EXEC-*` execution-path code changes · `FEE-MODEL-*` paper fee-model fidelity · `DEVNET-*` devnet routing / validation infra

---

## Critical path — recommended sequencing (post BITFOOT-DIP-SAMPLE + BITFOOT-2026-BASELINE + ANALYST-DISABLE, 2026-04-23)

**Paper bot state:** Speed-Demon-only (ANALYST-DISABLE-001 landed `cc8e5c9`; Analyst leak stopped). HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE-001 fix is deployed (24h verification window ends ~2026-04-23 23:00 UTC). BUG-022 (🔥 corrected_pnl_sol NULL on all post-reset rows) makes every paper-PnL number untrusted until fixed — that's the new #1 priority. Bitfoot strategy analysis has both needed verdicts (DIP-D + BASELINE-A directionally); ANALYST-POST-GRAD-001 unblocked for design-session kick-off.

1. ✅ **Session 1** (Sentry triage, `35bdfe6`), **Session 2 v2** (dashboard close-path, `5ac30cd`), **Session 2b** (entry INSERT, `dafe1fa`), **Session 3** (devnet/PumpPortal audit B-conditional, `fdd8aa8`), **Session 4** (LIVE-001 tune bundle), **EXEC-FIX** (EXEC-001 + EXEC-002 paired, `8073257`), **FEE-MODEL-001 FIX-2** (paper_trader corrected model, `e078b4c`), **FIX-1** (T5 rationale + CLEAN-003 + ML-012 investigation, `48c3097`), **GATES-V5** (ML-012 fix + 4 entry gates + stop-loss 0.20 + size caps, `1dec17b`), **MCP-RECON** (capabilities audit, `1e444bb` + `0c91492`), **DASH-RESET** (paper_trades archive + reset, `1176e12`), **Nansen v2 ship** (`c7f73ee`) + **Nansen Session A'** (payload shape fix, `c012475`).
2. ✅ **HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE-001** (`fc87b03` + `4c5508b`, 2026-04-22) — GeckoTerminal dict-schema fix + age-bypass for GATES-V5 HOLDER/BSR gates on fresh tokens. 24h verification window ends ~2026-04-23 23:00 UTC.
3. ✅ **ANALYST-DISABLE-001** (`cc8e5c9`, 2026-04-23) — governance Redis override closes the graduation-sniper bypass that the `ANALYST_DISABLED=true` env flag did not cover. Stops the 11.9% WR / -2.48 SOL / 17h leak.
4. ✅ **BITFOOT-DIP-SAMPLE-001** (`e053448`, 2026-04-23) — verdict DIP-D: 20.5% of retrievable unflagged pings hit 2x+; Bitfoot labels not reliable ground-truth.
5. ✅ **BITFOOT-2026-BASELINE** (`2b4cb73`, 2026-04-23) — verdict BASELINE-A directionally: 2-filter still concentrates winners in 2026 trending post-grad data (88.9% 2x+ on n=18, survivorship-inflated); Raydium post-grad vanished; Meteora up from 10% → 44% of winners.
6. 🟡 **BUG-022 INVESTIGATED** `ca4812d` (2026-04-28) — verdict 2a: writer never existed in committed code; only ever populated by a one-shot 2026-04-13 backfill script that was never committed and never re-ran. All 853 current closed rows NULL. **Important downgrade vs prior #1 framing:** because all current rows are post-`e078b4c` (FEE-MODEL-001), `realised_pnl_sol` is already authoritative — `corrected_pnl_sol` would be a `pass_through` identity copy. The "every paper-PnL number is biased" concern was overstated; directional findings are already correct. Fix is still recommended for symbolic correctness + ML training query safety: Option A (5-min one-time UPDATE + ~10-line inline close-time write). Audit doc: `docs/audits/CORRECTED_PNL_INVESTIGATION_2026_04_28.md`. **Fix execution: queued, ~30m next session.**
7. 📋 **ANALYST-PAPER-AUDIT-001** — 45m read-only diagnostic on the legacy `analyst` module that leaked -2.48 SOL in 17h. Determine retire-vs-retune; identify what re-enabled it on 2026-04-22. Prevents silent re-enablement.
8. 📋 **DOCS-004** — CLAUDE.md Vybe URL fix (`.com` → `.xyz`, 5m). Bundle with any other docs session or standalone.
9. 📋 **STATUS-CONVENTION-001** — ensure convention ✅ LANDED (prompt pasted + STATUS.md + seeded entries + template). Verify next session.
10. ⏪ **TUNE-005** ROLLED BACK 2026-04-29 — `HOLDER_COUNT_MIN` reverted 15 → 1 on signal_aggregator (was ✅ COMPLETED 2026-04-24, raising 1 → 15). Trigger: Speed Demon WR dropped 52.9% → 34.9% over 3 days post-TUNE-005 deploy. 24h validation window opens. Verified live: container swap 2026-04-29 09:27:58 UTC; new banner; zero HOLDER reject; cadence alive; no errors. Outcome: if WR recovers to ~50% baseline → codify rollback; if WR stays depressed → reapply TUNE-005 and look elsewhere for the regression cause.
11. 📋 **V5a — 1h intensive-supervised live window.** Replaces prior single-window LIVE-002. Gates on: paper cadence stable post-Analyst-disable (≥24h Speed-Demon-only); BUG-022 resolved (paper-PnL trustworthy); new T5a/T5b trigger definitions (T5-DESIGN-001 delivered via v5a prompt); ML-012 elif branch exercised in live mode (startup log "ML-012 FIX: ... ignoring override" present); first-live-trade fee_delta within ±0.005 SOL at 0.15-0.25 SOL sizing; stop_loss_20% exit string writes correctly; reconcile prep script cleans Redis paper state before flip. Wallet target 5 SOL.
12. 📋 **ANALYST-POST-GRAD-001** (multi-session, parallelizable to V5a) — revised filter spec per Phase-1 design summary at top of Tier 2 entry (DEX ∈ {PumpSwap, Meteora DAMM v2} — Raydium dropped; top-10 ≥30 + MC $50-300k; dex_paid + pre-grad vol/MC dropped; ROI calibrated from paper window).
13. 📋 **NANSEN-CLIENT-V2-MIGRATE-001** → **NANSEN-FEATURE-NORMALIZER-001** — Session B' split into Path A (caller migration) + Path B (ML normalizer); unblocks Nansen-powered features.
14. 📋 **V5b → V5c → V5d escalation**. Each stage gates on the prior stage completing cleanly. V5d (unsupervised) requires SEC-001 complete.
15. 📋 **SEC-001** (Redis + Postgres + Nansen rotation). Required before v5d. Waiver framework allows v5a-c under supervision per prior rollback doc §SEC-001.
16. 📋 **WALLET-REV-001**, **WHALE-001-v2**, **BITFOOT-ML-FEATURE-INTEGRATION-001** — edge-exploration work, parallelizable with v5 staged path (do not depend on v5 outcomes).
17. 📋 **BITFOOT-MONITOR-001** — 2-week prospective monitoring of fresh graduations (not retrospective trending_pools). Runs in parallel with anything. Its un-biased forward data is the only path to a real ROI calibration for ANALYST-POST-GRAD-001 (both DIP-D and BASELINE-A are biased; neither is forward-usable).

Rationale: paper pipeline is healthy (HOLDER fix lands + Analyst leak stopped), but paper-PnL trust is broken (BUG-022) — fixing it is cheap and gates every downstream observability-based decision. Bitfoot research has both verdicts landed → ANALYST-POST-GRAD-001 can begin design in parallel with other v5 prep. The hygiene / docs items (TUNE-005, DOCS-004, STATUS-CONVENTION-001, ANALYST-PAPER-AUDIT-001) are small and bundleable. V5a is the next live-enable gate, blocked on BUG-022 + stable ≥24h Speed-Demon-only paper cadence.

### LIVE-001 / Session 4 — T+24h gate outcome (appended 2026-04-20)

> **T+24h gate result (2026-04-20):** Strict gate FAIL on `stop_loss_35%` count-reduction criterion (23% reduction over 21.7h window vs 50% target); PASS on total-PnL criterion (+28% vs pro-rated baseline). **Jay-accepted** on PnL-up read. Env vars demonstrably took effect: `no_momentum` median hold_seconds dropped 81.1s → 51.2s (60s env var applied); TRAILING_STOP min peak_mult dropped 1.310 → 1.114 (+10% activation applied). Yellow flags: TRAILING_STOP WR dropped 20.9pp (91.8% → 70.9%) with per-trade avg PnL essentially flat; `no_momentum` per-trade loss worsened 33% (-0.058 → -0.080 SOL). Neither is a rollback trigger individually but both warrant continued observation in the second 24h window. Full assessment in `docs/audits/TUNE_T24H_GATE_2026_04_20.md`.

| FEE-MODEL-001 | Expand `paper_trader.fees_sol` calculation. Gap: paper `fees_sol` median is 0.503% of position size across all size buckets — models a single percentage fee only. Missing: (a) real platform fee (pump.fun is 1% each side = 2% round-trip, not 0.5%), (b) priority fee (0.001 SOL fixed per round-trip), (c) Jito tip (0.001-0.005 SOL fixed per round-trip), (d) realized slippage on 95.8% of trades (verified: `realised_pnl_sol = (exit/entry - 1) * amount - fees_sol` holds exactly on 6,087 of 6,352 closed trades). Impact: paper PnL overstates live by ~0.004 SOL/trade at current 0.05 SOL sizing (~8% of position). Break-even position size under realistic costs: 0.009 SOL @ 100% edge retention, 0.019 SOL @ 50%, 0.048 SOL @ 25%. Current `MIN_POSITION_SOL=0.05` sits at the pessimistic break-even — defensible for supervised windows, tight for unsupervised. Fix shape: parameterize as `(pct_platform + pct_lp) * 2 * amount + priority_fee * 2 + jito_tip * 2 + slippage_realized * amount`; env vars per component so real-world calibration feeds back without code changes. **Priority escalation 2026-04-20 (post-Session-5-v4):** first live data point proved the paper fee model understates live by ~96× on pre-grad pump.fun round-trips. Single trade on mint `yh3n441...` at 0.365 SOL showed -0.094 SOL on-chain (25.8% of position) vs +0.002 SOL paper prediction. Dominant gap is slippage (~22.5% of position), not fixed fees. Escalated from Tier 2 (paper fidelity improvement) to **Tier 1 PRE-LIVE BLOCKER**: all Session 5 v5+ live windows blocked until paper model is recalibrated and historical paper edge re-baselined under corrected model. FIX-2 session (commit `e078b4c`) implemented the fix in `services/paper_trader.py` + rebaseline in `docs/audits/PAPER_EDGE_REBASELINE_2026_04_20.md`. SLIPPAGE-CALIBRATION-001 is the ongoing operational loop to refine coefficients from live data. | ✅ COMPLETED `e078b4c` (Tier 1 PRE-LIVE BLOCKER) | 45-60m CC + 7d paper obs recalibration | paper-live edge parity + v5 sizing inputs | EXEC-003 (for default values) | chat-layer 2026-04-20 fee-model analysis; `docs/audits/PAPER_EDGE_REBASELINE_2026_04_20.md` |

| SLIPPAGE-CALIBRATION-001 | Ongoing slippage calibration from live data. FEE-MODEL-001 (FIX-2, commit `e078b4c`) ships a first-cut size-aware slippage model based on a SINGLE live data point (v4 rollback: -0.094 SOL on 0.365 SOL pre-grad). Better than the old flat model but unlikely to be correct in the tail. As more live trades accumulate, recalibrate: (1) pull all closed live trades; (2) compute `observed_slippage = actual_exit_price - expected_exit_price` per trade; (3) regress against `(amount_sol, bonding_curve_progress, pool)` to produce updated coefficients for `SLIPPAGE_RANGES`; (4) update env vars `PAPER_FEE_*` and in-code `SLIPPAGE_RANGES` tuples. No code change required to the simulator structure — FIX-2 makes everything env-overridable. This is an operational tuning loop, not a bug fix. Recommended cadence: monthly or per 10+ live trades accumulated. | 📋 QUEUED (recurring) | 30m per calibration pass | paper-live edge parity improves over time | FEE-MODEL-001 ✅ | `docs/audits/SESSION_5_V4_ROLLBACK_FINDINGS.md`, `docs/audits/PAPER_EDGE_REBASELINE_2026_04_20.md` |

(2) BITFOOT-2026-BASELINE (`docs/audits/BITFOOT_2026_BASELINE_2026_04_23.md`) — 2-filter Bitfoot (top10 ≥30 + MC $50-300k) still concentrates winners in 2026 trending post-grad data (88.9% 2x+ on n=18, bias-inflated) → edge persists directionally. **Required revisions for design:** (a) DROP `dex_paid 🔴` rule — untestable on current stack, no signal source on GT free tier; (b) DROP pre-grad `vol/MC <1.5` gate — un-replicable without Bitfoot-style pre-grad visibility, and the h24 proxy rejects actual winners (NORMIE 29x / Nintondo 33x / RND 17x all had h24 vol/MC >1.5); (c) EXPECT Meteora to be a meaningful share (44% of 2026 winner set vs 10% of 2025 dataset) — ensure Meteora DAMM v2 routing is validated in execution layer; (d) Raydium absent from 2026 post-grad trending (0/42, vs 39% in 2025) — de-prioritize Raydium entry allocation; (e) ROI must be calibrated from live paper window, not historical Bitfoot math — do NOT use 88.9% hit rate as a forward expectation. See both deliverables' §6 for full guidance. **Bitfoot-inspired Analyst personality for post-graduation Solana tokens** (multi-session build). Strategy shape (from 32,851-ping 10.3-month Bitfoot Era-1 dataset, 2025-01→2025-12, loaded at `session_outputs/bitfoot_analysis/`): **Entry filter — three counterintuitive rules, robust across H1+H2 2025:** (1) Top-10 holder concentration ≥ 30% (higher concentration predicts BETTER outcomes; 32.2% 2x-hit-rate vs 28.7% baseline, stable across both halves); (2) Volume/Market-Cap ratio < 1.5 (low pre-ping turnover is better; vol/MC <0.5 → 35% 2x rate vs vol/MC >8 → 18%); (3) Dex Paid = 🔴 (unpaid) or ignore Dex Paid (paid is an anti-signal — mean peak 1.96x paid vs 2.79x unpaid). **Additional hard filters:** Age 30-300s post-graduation, MC $50-300k, DEX ∈ {PumpSwap, Raydium, Meteora}. **Entry window:** wait 30-60s after detection to verify (fast <1min pumps UNDERPERFORM slow 1-30min pumps; no arms race needed — 83% of total profit capturable with 2-min reaction time, 93% with 1-min). **Exit logic:** staged TP (50% at 2x, 25% at 5x, 25% loose trail); hold duration HOURS not seconds (median time-to-peak 30min; 10-20x median 2.1h; 50-100x median 10h; 100x+ median 1.2d); 24h time-stop; 50% stop-loss. **Sizing:** fixed 0.2-0.5 SOL per trade; Kelly-inspired f\* ≈ 0.05-0.10 wallet fraction; max 10-20 concurrent positions (higher than Speed Demon because hold is longer). **Expected performance (rough, pending BITFOOT-DIP-SAMPLE-001 verification):** ~30-50 trades/mo, +$600-2000/mo under mid-range assumptions; ROI ±30% depending on what the 71% unflagged pings actually did. **Dependencies:** Helius graduation detection (already in signal pipeline), Vybe for top-10 / volume enrichment (free tier sufficient), independent graduation signal source (does NOT depend on Bitfoot Telegram subscription — replicates filter heuristics on own pipeline, bypasses adverse-selection problem of being Nth-in-line). Can be built as a new personality module in signal_aggregator (parallel to Speed Demon, doesn't interfere). Initial deploy as paper-only, observe 2 weeks, decide on live activation. **Sub-sessions:** (a) graduation detection confirmation + filter logic scaffold in signal_aggregator, (b) exit logic extension in bot_core to handle hours-long holds + staged TP variant, (c) paper-mode activation + observation instrumentation, (d) dashboard widget for Analyst-Post-Grad perf separate from Speed Demon. | 📋 QUEUED (multi-session) | 4-6 CC sessions | **highest-return new strategy** based on 10mo labeled dataset | BITFOOT-DIP-SAMPLE-001 (informs ROI confidence), HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE-001 (if Analyst uses same holder-count feed) | `session_outputs/bitfoot_analysis/` (dataset + scripts); chat 2026-04-22 FINDINGS_ML.md + FINDINGS_TIME_TO_PEAK.md |

| DEPLOY-DISCIPLINE-001 | Railway auto-deploy latency investigation. Session 5 v4 attempt: Railway `set-variables` at 20:35:57 UTC did not trigger `bot_core` redeploy until ~20:45 (~10 min latency vs typical 60-90s). Known Railway behavior — env-var changes do not always trigger immediate redeploy. For live-window sessions where timing matters, choose one of: (a) use `railway up -s bot_core` explicitly after env change to force redeploy (conflicts with CLAUDE.md "no railway up AND git push in same session" — would need rule carve-out); (b) monitor Railway MCP deploy status polling immediately after `set-variables` to detect whether a redeploy fires, fall back to `railway up` if not; (c) document the observed behavior in CLAUDE.md so future Session 5 prompts account for variable-set-to-redeploy latency. ---

## Operating principles (preserved from prior roadmap)

- **One substantive lever per session** — multiple parallel changes make failure attribution impossible
- **Verification windows BEFORE tuning** (24h+ minimum) — don't tune without observation data
- **All deploys must have auto-revert conditions** — `git revert <hash>` is the rollback
- **All thresholds env-var-configurable** for kill switch — never hardcode trading parameters
- **Read-only diagnostic prompts BEFORE write prompts** on ambiguous items
- **Never deploy multiple Railway services simultaneously** (per CLAUDE.md)
- **No `railway up` AND `git push` in the same session** (duplicate deploys waste build minutes)
- **Update this roadmap at the end of every session** — append a changelog entry

---

## Review cadence

- **Daily during active deploy weeks** — check top-3 priority Tier 1 items
- **Weekly when stable** — review all 📋 QUEUED + ⏸️ DEFERRED items, re-date or promote
- **Triggered** — when a `Depends on` clears, re-evaluate that item immediately

Items sitting in ⏸️ DEFERRED for 30+ days without a status change get either DROPPED or re-scheduled with a new trigger. No drift.

---

- **2026-04-21** (DASH-RESET detail amendment to prior GATES-V5+MCP-RECON+DASH-RESET consolidation) — Follow-up to commit `057f938` (earlier this day) after DASH-RESET deliverable details became available. **DASH-RESET specifics (commit `1176e12`):** `paper_trades` archived to `paper_trades_archive_20260421` with **6,635 rows** preserved; **6,629** `trade_mode='paper'` rows DELETEd; **6 live rows (IDs 6575-6580, all closed)** intentionally preserved untouched; new baseline `portfolio_snapshots` row (`id=39038`) written at 20.0 SOL; Redis `bot:portfolio:balance` + `bot:status` cleared and rewritten at baseline. **Procedural finding:** required **3 bot_core redeploy iterations** to land the baseline cleanly due to a race between the DELETE+baseline-INSERT SQL and bot_core's 5-min portfolio-snapshot cycle — the running bot_core would snapshot the transient post-DELETE state before the baseline INSERT committed, overwriting the baseline. Clean sequence (to codify in CLAUDE.md for future resets): (1) DELETE paper rows, (2) baseline INSERT in same transaction, (3) nudge bot_core redeploy within 60s of the INSERT to force a fresh `_load_state` read, (4) verify `bot:portfolio:balance=20.0` via Redis GET before the next 5-min tick. **Two new Tier 1 items surfaced by reset outcomes:** **BUG-021** (20m — `daily_pnl_sol` writer in `bot_core.py:1963-1987` and `api_paper_stats` in `dashboard_api.py:1148-1159` aggregate paper_trades without filtering `trade_mode`; post-reset the 6 preserved live rows' -3.205 SOL leaks into "paper" aggregates until paper trades accumulate. Pre-existing bug, surfaced by the shrunk paper aggregate); **CLEAN-004** (10m — bot_core restores `consecutive_losses=4` from both Postgres `bot_state` and Redis `bot:consecutive_losses=4` on every restart; one live loss in v5 trips the sell-storm circuit breaker at 5+ unnecessarily. Pre-v5-flip reset: `UPDATE bot_state SET value_text='0' WHERE key='consecutive_losses'` + `DEL bot:consecutive_losses`. Add to `scripts/live_flip_prep.sh` so every future flip resets the counter). Zero items dropped, reordered, renamed, or merged. All pre-existing items preserved. Docs-only diff.
- **2026-04-22 (later — HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE fix lands + BUG-021 partial + CLEAN-004 reset)** — After Jay's roadmap consolidation (prior entry), dedicated fix session landed. **HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE-001 ✅ FIXED** via two commits: (1) `fc87b03` — GeckoTerminal `/tokens/{mint}/info` endpoint schema change from bare int to dict `{"count": N, "distribution_percentage": {...}, "last_updated": "..."}` broke `int(attrs.get("holders", 0))` at two call sites (`_fetch_gecko_pool_data` L782 + `_process_graduations` L2441). `int(dict)` raises TypeError, caught silently by outer `except Exception`, `holders` stays 0. Fixed with isinstance(dict) branch reading `.count`. Post-deploy: `GRAD_ACCEPT: 61VJc9L1Xekp score=70 holders=198 kol=0 whale=1.00` at 13:39:15 UTC confirmed graduation path working. (2) `4c5508b` — age-bypass for HOLDER + BSR gates when `token_age_seconds < GATES_V5_MIN_AGE_SEC` (default 30). Rationale: fresh pump.fun new_token signals at age=0s legitimately have no GeckoTerminal data yet, no token:stats populated yet. Gate rejecting `0 < 1` is meaningless — the gate exists to filter "no organic interest", not "data hasn't arrived yet". PRE_FILTER_SCORE_MIN=1.15 is NOT age-bypassed because `pre_filter_score = position_size_multiplier` is calculable at age=0s. New env var `GATES_V5_MIN_AGE_SEC`. Audit doc: `docs/audits/HOLDER_PIPELINE_FIX_2026_04_22.md`. **BUG-021 🟡 PARTIAL** via `bc622eb` — dashboard_api sites (`api_paper_stats` + `api_portfolio_history`) now apply `trade_mode` filter via `_get_mode(request)`. Paper-view excludes live rows; live-view selects `market_mode='LIVE_ONCHAIN'` snapshots. Response body now includes `"mode": "paper"\|"live"` for caller verification. `services/bot_core.py:1963-1987` `_portfolio_snapshot_task` write-path deferred (still writes `daily_pnl_sol` unfiltered). **CLEAN-004 ✅ RESET** — Redis `bot:consecutive_losses` set to 0; Postgres `bot_state.consecutive_losses` updated to `'0'`. Follow-up script update pending (add to `scripts/live_flip_prep.sh`). Status changes: HOLDER-DATA-PIPELINE-001 📋 → ✅ COMPLETED; BUG-021 📋 → 🟡 PARTIAL; CLEAN-004 📋 → ✅ COMPLETED (with script follow-up). ID scheme unchanged. - **2026-04-29** (LIVE-FEE-MODEL-AUDIT — read-only paper/live divergence check, verdict MAJOR DIVERGENCE) — Read-only audit comparing `services/execution.py` (live) vs `services/paper_trader.py` (paper) for slippage, fees, PnL formula, TP/SL trigger, sizing, and `features_json`. Plus empirical closed-form check on 6 historical live rows from `paper_trades`. **Verdict: MAJOR DIVERGENCE.** Four load-bearing differences: (1) live PnL formula at `services/bot_core.py:1232` is `(exit/entry-1)*amt` with **no `- fees` term**; paper subtracts fees explicitly. (2) Live writes `slippage_pct=0.0` and `fees_sol=0.0` on every paper_trades row (entry INSERT and close UPDATE both omit those columns). Verified empirically — all 6 live rows have both columns at exactly 0.0. (3) Live entry/exit prices are queried RPC prices, not actual fill prices — `execute_trade` returns no fee/price data; bot_core calls `_get_token_price` after success. (4) Live `features_json` is NULL on all 6 historical live rows. **Closed-form check on 4 live rows with valid prices:** all 4 match `(exit/entry-1)*amt` (no fee subtraction) to ≤ 1e-5 SOL. STOP condition (>1 row mismatched >1e-3 SOL) NOT tripped — divergence is consistent across all rows. id=6580 v4 yh3n441 trade explained: paper recorded +0.0019 SOL; on-chain actual −0.094 SOL; FEE-MODEL-001 corrected paper model predicted −0.094 within ±0.02. **TP/SL trigger logic = parity** (single code path). **Sizing logic = parity** (`risk_manager.calculate_position_size`). **V5a wallet math (carry):** `_max_pos = min(MAX_POSITION_SOL=1.50, wallet * MAX_POSITION_SOL_FRACTION=0.10)`. - **2026-04-30** (BUG-022-HOTFIX — distinct param slots for corrected_* columns; Session B follow-up) — Bot_core post Session-B redeploy threw `ERROR: Exit check error for speed_demon:<mint>: inconsistent types deduced for parameter $10` on every exit attempt. Three trade IDs (7743/7744/7745) loop-failed for ~2 min before fix landed. Root cause: BUG-022 inline-write reused $4/$5/$10 for both realised_* and corrected_* columns; asyncpg prepared-statement protocol cant deduce a single PostgreSQL type when the same param is referenced for columns of different declared types (schema has `outcome` as character varying; corrected_outcome as text or similar divergence). Fix `17c2aac`: pass each value twice with distinct param slots — paper_trader.py uses $11/$12/$13 for corrected_*; bot_core.py staged-TP correction uses $5/$6/$7. Compile-checked. Single push triggered bot_core auto-redeploy. Backfill (1111 rows from `392c928`) is unaffected — that was a separate ad-hoc UPDATE without parameter reuse. **Lesson preserved:** chain prompt asserted "param reuse is valid PostgreSQL" — true in raw psql, false for asyncpg with prepared statements when param appears in columns of different declared types. Future inline-write changes that touch dual-write should use distinct slots even if it costs 3 extra Python args. ID scheme unchanged. Zero items dropped.

- **2026-04-30** (SD-MC-CEILING attempt #1 ⏪ ROLLED BACK — design flaw discovered in verification; SD_MC_CEILING_002 follow-up queued) — Step 5 verification (~30 min post-deploy) found 2 of 14 fresh SD trades since 08:01 UTC entered with `market_cap_at_entry > 3000` (id 7749 at $4,482 entered 08:10:50 UTC; id 7757 at $9,807 entered 08:28:00 UTC — both definitively after SA container swap at ~08:08 UTC per build timestamp 08:03:40 UTC). Root cause: gate reads `raw_data.get("usdMarketCap", raw_data.get("market_cap_usd", 0))` which is `0` at signal-time for fresh pump.fun new_token events (visible in FILTER logs as `mc=$0`). The actual MC stored in `paper_trades.market_cap_at_entry` is computed in bot_core at entry-time as `entry_price * 1_000_000_000` (total supply) where entry_price derives from BC reserves (`vSolInBondingCurve / vTokensInBondingCurve` * SOL_USD). Gate reads the wrong source — structurally inert for the dominant SD signal source (fresh new_token signals from pumpportal). Not a code bug; design flaw in the chain prompts gate placement. **Rollback executed:** `SD_MC_CEILING_USD=999999999` set on signal_aggregator via Railway MCP. Code retained as harmless no-op at 999M threshold; re-enable when proper fix lands. **Follow-up SD_MC_CEILING_002:** Option (a) move gate to bot_core at entry decision (uses actual MC; gate placement closer to truth but later in pipeline) OR Option (b) compute MC from BC reserves in SA gate (mirrors bot_core; matches chain prompts intent of filtering at signal-gate stage; introduces dependency on `market:sol_price` Redis key in SA gating path). Recommend (b). ETA ~30m next session. **Status changes:** SD_MC_CEILING_001 ✅ DEPLOYED → ⏪ ROLLED BACK 2026-04-30. SD_MC_CEILING_002 📋 NEW (deferred follow-up). All other pre-existing items unchanged. ID scheme extended: SD_MC_CEILING_002. Zero items dropped, reordered, renamed, or merged. **Audit doc:** `docs/audits/SD_MC_CEILING_DEPLOY_2026_04_30.md` (updated §5 with verification fail + rollback record + proper-fix options).
